responses. Lower values lead to more predictable and typical responses, while higher values encourage more diverse and less common responses. At 0, the model always gives the same response for a given input.</p>

probabilities add up to P. A lower value makes the model's responses more predictable, while the default setting allows for a full range of token choices. Think of it like a dynamic Top-K.</p>

line-clamp-2 md:line-clamp-1 text-sm text-slate-10 mb-2 mt-0.5 md:mb-0"><p>Consider only the top tokens with "sufficiently high" probabilities based on the probability of the most likely token. Think of it like a dynamic Top-P. A lower Top-A value focuses the choices based on the highest probability token but with a narrower scope. A higher Top-A value does not necessarily affect the creativity of the output, but rather refines the filtering process based on the maximum probability.</p>

min-w-min" data-state="closed"><div class="text-xs text-slate-10">p50</div><div class="text-lg text-slate-11">0</div></div><div class="flex w-auto flex-col items-center gap-1 min-w-min" data-state="closed"><div class="text-xs text-slate-10">p90</div><div class="text-lg text-slate-11">0</div></div></div></td></tr><tr class="text-lg h-24 border-t border-border/50 first:border-t-0"><td class="w-2/3 py-4 align-top"><div class="flex flex-col gap-1"><div class="flex items-center gap-6"><div class="text-md text-slate-9"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" fill="none" viewBox="0 0 24 24" stroke-width="1.5" stroke="currentColor" aria-hidden="true" data-slot="icon" class="size-4"><path stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" d="M15 13.5H9m4.06-7.19-2.12-2.12a1.5 1.5 0 0 0-1.061-.44H4.5A2.25 2.25 0 0 0 2.25 6v12a2.25 2.25 0 0 0 2.25 2.25h15A2.25 2.25 0 0 0 21.75 18V9a2.25 2.25 0 0 0-2.25-2.25h-5.379a1.5 1.5 0 0 1-1.06-.44Z"></path></svg></div><div class="text-lg text-slate-12">repetition_penalty</div></div><div class="flex gap-1"><div class="prose-slate prose-hr:border-current prose-table:min-w-full prose-table:overflow-hidden prose-table:rounded-lg prose-table:border prose-table:border-current prose-ol:list-decimal prose-ol:pl-8 prose-ul:list-disc prose-ul:pl-8 prose-ol:pb-4 prose-ul:pb-4 prose-li:whitespace-normal prose-th:border prose-th:border-current prose-th:px-4 prose-th:py-2 prose-td:border prose-td:border-current prose-td:px-4 prose-td:py-2 prose-h3:font-medium prose-h3:text-current prose-p:break-words prose-p:leading-6 tracking-tight line-clamp-2 md:line-clamp-1 text-sm text-slate-10 mb-2 mt-0.5 md:mb-0"><p>Helps to reduce the repetition of tokens from the input. A higher value makes the model less likely to repeat tokens, but too high a value can make the output less coherent (often with run-on sentences that lack small words). Token penalty scales based on original token's probability.</p>
<ul>
<li>
<p>Optional, <strong>float</strong>, 0.0 to 2.0</p>
</li>
<li>
<p>Default: 1.0</p>
</li>
<li>
<p>Explainer Video: <a href="https://youtu.be/LHjGAnLm3DM" class="underline underline-offset-2" target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer">Watch<svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" fill="none" viewBox="0 0 24 24" stroke-width="1.5" stroke="currentColor" aria-hidden="true" data-slot="icon" class="ml-1 inline-block w-4"><path stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" d="M13.5 6H5.25A2.25 2.25 0 0 0 3 8.25v10.5A2.25 2.25 0 0 0 5.25 21h10.5A2.25 2.25 0 0 0 18 18.75V10.5m-10.5 6L21 3m0 0h-5.25M21 3v5.25"></path></svg></a></p>
</li>
</ul></div><button class="inline-flex items-center justify-center whitespace-nowrap rounded-md font-medium transition-colors focus-visible:outline-none disabled:pointer-events-none disabled:opacity-50 focus-visible:ring-1 focus-visible:ring-ring gap-2 leading-6 text-muted-foreground hover:bg-accent hover:text-accent-foreground h-6 w-6 shrink-0"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" fill="none" viewBox="0 0 24 24" stroke-width="1.5" stroke="currentColor" aria-hidden="true" data-slot="icon" class="size-4 text-muted-foreground transition-transform duration-200"><path stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" d="m19.5 8.25-7.5 7.5-7.5-7.5"></path></svg></button></div></div></td><td class="pt-6 pl-6 align-top"><div class="flex justify-between w-full"><div class="flex w-auto flex-col min-w-min" data-state="closed"><div class="text-xs text-slate-10">p50</div><div class="text-lg text-slate-11">1</div></div><div class="flex w-auto flex-col items-center gap-1 min-w-min" data-state="closed"><div class="text-xs text-slate-10">p90</div><div class="text-lg text-slate-11">1</div></div></div></td></tr><tr class="text-lg h-24 border-t border-border/50 first:border-t-0"><td class="w-2/3 py-4 align-top"><div class="flex flex-col gap-1"><div class="flex items-center gap-6"><div class="text-md text-slate-9"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" fill="none" viewBox="0 0 24 24" stroke-width="1.5" stroke="currentColor" aria-hidden="true" data-slot="icon" class="size-4"><path stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" d="M3 4.5h14.25M3 9h9.75M3 13.5h5.25m5.25-.75L17.25 9m0 0L21 12.75M17.25 9v12"></path></svg></div><div class="text-lg text-slate-12">min_p</div></div><div class="flex gap-1"><div class="prose-slate prose-hr:border-current prose-table:min-w-full prose-table:overflow-hidden prose-table:rounded-lg prose-table:border prose-table:border-current prose-ol:list-decimal prose-ol:pl-8 prose-ul:list-disc prose-ul:pl-8 prose-ol:pb-4 prose-ul:pb-4 prose-li:whitespace-normal prose-th:border prose-th:border-current prose-th:px-4 prose-th:py-2 prose-td:border prose-td:border-current prose-td:px-4 prose-td:py-2 prose-h3:font-medium prose-h3:text-current prose-p:break-words prose-p:leading-6 tracking-tight line-clamp-2 md:line-clamp-1 text-sm text-slate-10 mb-2 mt-0.5 md:mb-0"><p>Represents the minimum probability for a token to be
considered, relative to the probability of the most likely token. (The value changes depending on the confidence level of the most probable token.) If your Min-P is set to 0.1, that means it will only allow for tokens that are at least 1/10th as probable as the best possible option.</p>
<ul>
<li>
<p>Optional, <strong>float</strong>, 0.0 to 1.0</p>
</li>
<li>
<p>Default: 0.0</p>
</li>
</ul></div><button class="inline-flex items-center justify-center whitespace-nowrap rounded-md font-medium transition-colors focus-visible:outline-none disabled:pointer-events-none disabled:opacity-50 focus-visible:ring-1 focus-visible:ring-ring gap-2 leading-6 text-muted-foreground hover:bg-accent hover:text-accent-foreground h-6 w-6 shrink-0"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" fill="none" class="w-2/3 py-4 align-top"><div class="flex flex-col gap-1"><div class="flex items-center gap-6"><div class="text-md text-slate-9"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" fill="none" viewBox="0 0 24 24" stroke-width="1.5" stroke="currentColor" aria-hidden="true" data-slot="icon" class="size-4"><path stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" d="M3 13.125C3 12.504 3.504 12 4.125 12h2.25c.621 0 1.125.504 1.125 1.125v6.75C7.5 20.496 6.996 21 6.375 21h-2.25A1.125 1.125 0 0 1 3 19.875v-6.75ZM9.75 8.625c0-.621.504-1.125 1.125-1.125h2.25c.621 0 1.125.504 1.125 1.125v11.25c0 .621-.504 1.125-1.125 1.125h-2.25a1.125 1.125 0 0 1-1.125-1.125V8.625ZM16.5 4.125c0-.621.504-1.125 1.125-1.125h2.25C20.496 3 21 3.504 21 4.125v15.75c0 .621-.504 1.125-1.125 1.125h-2.25a1.125 1.125 0 0 1-1.125-1.125V4.125Z"></path></svg></div><div class="text-lg text-slate-12">top_a</div></div><div class="flex gap-1"><div class="prose-slate prose-hr:border-current prose-table:min-w-full prose-table:overflow-hidden prose-table:rounded-lg prose-table:border prose-table:border-current prose-ol:list-decimal prose-ol:pl-8 prose-ul:list-disc prose-ul:pl-8 prose-ol:pb-4 prose-ul:pb-4 prose-li:whitespace-normal prose-th:border prose-th:border-current prose-th:px-4 prose-th:py-2 prose-td:border prose-td:border-current prose-td:px-4 prose-td:py-2 prose-h3:font-medium prose-h3:text-current prose-p:break-words prose-p:leading-6 tracking-tight line-clamp-2 md:line-clamp-1 text-sm text-slate-10 mb-2 mt-0.5 md:mb-0"><p>Consider only the top tokens with "sufficiently high" probabilities based on the probability of the most likely token. Think of it like a dynamic Top-P. A lower Top-A value focuses the choices based on the highest probability token but with a narrower scope. A higher Top-A value does not necessarily affect the creativity of the output, but rather refines the filtering process based on the maximum probability.</p>

<li>
<p>Optional, <strong>float</strong>, 0.0 to 1.0</p>
</li>
<li>
<p>Default: 0.0</p>
</li>

DeepSeek V3<a class="opacity-0 transition-opacity duration-200 group-hover:opacity-100" href="/deepseek/deepseek-chat/uptime"><button class="inline-flex items-center justify-center whitespace-nowrap across all providers</h3></div><div class="flex flex-col items-start gap-4"><div class="h-80 w-full overflow-hidden rounded-lg border border-border"><iframe title="uptime graph" height="318"></iframe></div><p>When an error occurs in an upstream provider, we recover by routing to another healthy provider.<br>If a model only has one host or the request filters only match a single provider, the request is "irrecoverable."</p><div class="h-80 w-full overflow-hidden rounded-lg border border-border"><iframe title="error recovery graph" src="https://us5.datadoghq.com/graph/embed?token=dde50516dc7ac8620196149a1bdb230cbdb7db085efd8d3fd316477d200db354&amp;legend=true&amp;height=318&amp;width=718" width="718" height="318"></iframe></div><p><a href="/docs/provider-routing">Learn more</a> about our load balancing and customization options.</p></div></div></div><div data-orientation="horizontal" role="none" class="shrink-0 bg-border/50 h-px w-full my-4 last:opacity-0"></div><div class="py-8"><div class="flex w-full flex-col"><div class="group flex flex-col gap-2 pb-3 text-left"><h2 class="relative flex items-center justify-start gap-2"><span id="api" class="absolute -top-40"></span>Sample code and API for DeepSeek V3<a class="opacity-0 transition-opacity duration-200 group-hover:opacity-100" prose-li:whitespace-normal prose-th:border prose-th:border-current prose-th:px-4 prose-th:py-2 prose-td:border prose-td:border-current prose-td:px-4 prose-td:py-2 prose-h3:font-medium prose-h3:text-current prose-p:break-words tracking-tight line-clamp-3 text-xs text-slate-9 prose-p:leading-4"><p>DeepSeek-Coder-V2, an open-source Mixture-of-Experts (MoE) code language model. It is further pre-trained from an intermediate checkpoint of DeepSeek-V2 with additional 6 trillion tokens.</p>
<p>The original V1 model was trained from scratch on 2T tokens, with a composition of 87% code and 13% natural language in both English and Chinese. It was pre-trained on project-level code corpus by employing a extra fill-in-the-blank task.</p></div></a></div><div role="group" aria-roledescription="slide" class="min-w-0 shrink-0 grow-0 pl-4 basis-1/1"><a class="group flex h-full w-64 shrink-0 flex-col justify-between space-y-2 rounded-md border px-4 py-4 text-left shadow-sm md:w-80" href="/deepseek/deepseek-chat-v2.5"><div class="mb-2 line-clamp-1 text-lg font-medium text-slate-11 group-hover:text-accent-foreground group-hover:underline">DeepSeek V2.5</div><div class="prose-slate prose-hr:border-current prose-table:min-w-full prose-table:overflow-hidden prose-table:rounded-lg prose-table:border prose-table:border-current prose-ol:list-decimal prose-ol:pl-8 prose-ul:list-disc prose-ul:pl-8 prose-ol:pb-4 prose-ul:pb-4 prose-li:whitespace-normal prose-th:border prose-th:border-current prose-th:px-4 prose-th:py-2 prose-td:border prose-td:border-current prose-td:px-4 prose-td:py-2 prose-h3:font-medium prose-h3:text-current prose-p:break-words tracking-tight line-clamp-3 text-xs text-slate-9 prose-p:leading-4"><p>DeepSeek-V2.5 is an upgraded version that combines DeepSeek-V2-Chat and DeepSeek-Coder-V2-Instruct.
